	$(".ParticipateEvent").click(function (){
		var eventID = $(this).attr("href");
		// Login
		FB.login(function (response)
		{
			//console.log(response);
			if (response.authResponse) {
            	//console.log(response); // dump complete info
            	access_token = response.authResponse.accessToken; //get access token
            	user_id = response.authResponse.userID; //get FB UID
			
				FB.api("/"+eventID+"/attending", 'POST', {attending: true}, function (response){
					if(typeof(response.error) == "undefined")
					{
						window.alert("Voc&ecirc; est&aacute; confirmado no evento");
					}
				})
			
        	} else {
            	console.log('User cancelled login or did not fully authorize.');
        	}   
		}, 	{ scope: 'publish_stream,user_events,rsvp_event' })
		// Login
		//console.log(eventID);
		return false;
	})
	</script>

	<h3 class="titleBlock icnSpriteBefore"><a href="/enderecos/">Endereços</a></h3>
	<div class="widgetBlock">
		<div class="texts">
			<h3>Endereços da <br />Igreja Universal</h3>
			<p>Confira as igrejas mais próximas a você ou pesquise uma igreja por endereço.</p>
		</div>
		<form name="frmcontrol" id="frmcontrol" action="#" method="POST">
			<input type="hidden" name="widgetadd" id="widgetadd" value="1" />
			<input type="text" name="ctbusca" id="ctbusca" class="search" placeholder="Busque por Estado, Cidade ou Endereço" />
			<button type="button" onclick="enviaForm()">buscar</button>
		</form>
	</div>
</div>
<script>
	function strip_tags(input, allowed) {
		allowed = (((allowed.replace(/</g, '< ') || '') + '').toLowerCase().match(/<[a-z][a-z0-9]*>/g) || []).join('');
		var tags = /<\/?([a-z][a-z0-9]*)\b[^>]*>/gi, commentsAndPhpTags = /<!--[\s\S]*?-->|<\?(?:php)?[\s\S]*?\?>/gi;
		return input.replace(/>/g, '> ').replace(commentsAndPhpTags, '').replace(tags, function ($0, $1) {
			return allowed.indexOf('<' + $1.toLowerCase() + '>') > -1 ? $0 : '';
		});
	}
	function removeacento(strToReplace) {
		str_acento= 'áàãâäéèêëíìîïóòõôöúùûüçÁÀÃÂÄÉÈÊËÍÌÎÏÓÒÕÖÔÚÙÛÜÇ';
		str_sem_acento = 'aaaaaeeeeiiiiooooouuuucAAAAAEEEEIIIIOOOOOUUUUC';
		var nova='';
		for (var i = 0; i < strToReplace.length; i++) {
			if (str_acento.indexOf(strToReplace.charAt(i)) != -1)
				nova+=str_sem_acento.substr(str_acento.search(strToReplace.substr(i,1)),1);
			else
				nova+=strToReplace.substr(i,1);
			}
		return nova;
	}
	
	$('.search').keypress(function(event){
		if((event.keyCode ? event.keyCode : event.which) == '13') {
			if($(this).val() != '') {
				$('#frmcontrol').attr('action', 'http://www.universal.org/enderecos/busca/'+removeacento(strip_tags($(this).val(),'').trim()).replace(/ /g,'-').toLowerCase()+'/');
				$('#ctbusca').val(strip_tags($(this).val(), ''));
				$('#frmcontrol').submit();
			}
			else
			location = 'http://www.universal.org/enderecos/';
			return false;
		}
	});
	function enviaForm(){
		$('#frmcontrol').attr('action', 'http://www.universal.org/enderecos/busca/'+removeacento(strip_tags($("#ctbusca").val(),'').trim()).replace(/ /g,'-').toLowerCase()+'/');
		$('#ctbusca').val(strip_tags($("#ctbusca").val(), ''));
		$('#frmcontrol').submit();
	}
</script>  <!-- Blocks Bottom -->
